## Determine what I no longer need
- We don't need `bams_no-dedup/`
- We don't need `FastQC_no-dedup/`
- `#NOTE` Remember to generate this type of file, warnings_alignTranscriptsPerReadNmax.txt, for the recent UMI-extracted datasets

<details>
<summary><i>Code: Determine what I no longer need</i></summary>

```bash
#!/bin/bash
#DONTRUN #CONTINUE

.,
., bams_no-dedup/*
., bams_no-dedup/*/*
rmr bams_no-dedup/

., FastQC_no-dedup/
., FastQC_no-dedup/*
., FastQC_no-dedup/*/*
rmr FastQC_no-dedup/

cd fastqs_no-dedup/symlinks \
	|| echo "cd'ing failed; check on this..."

for i in *.gz; do unlink "${i}"; done

cd ..
rmdir symlinks/

cd trim_galore \
	|| echo "cd'ing failed; check on this..."
.,
rm *.{txt,gz}

cd ..
rmdir trim_galore/

cd ..
rmdir fastqs_no-dedup/

.,

mv tests/ test_tutorial/

mv tutorials/* test_tutorial/

rmdir tutorials/

mv miscellaneous/ cleaning/

mkdir initial/
mv work_draft_process-data_4tU-seq_fastqs_initial.md initial/

mv cleaning/ etc_cleaning/
mv initial/ etc_initial/

.,

#  QC will be organized in a different way, so...
rmdir FastQC_UMI-dedup/

mkdir etc_QC/

git mv work_draft_QC-etc.md work_run-QC.md etc_QC/

#  Move this notebook into etc_cleaning/
git mv work_clean-up.md etc_cleaning/
```
</details>
